BEGIN
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Osobas](
    [OsobaID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [PartnerID] [int] NULL,
    [PartnerCentralaID] [int] NULL,
    [Lozinka] [varchar](30) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [PartnerGrupa] [varchar](20) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Ime] [varchar](30) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Prezime] [varchar](30) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [PartnerNaziv] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Adresa] [varchar](200) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [PostBroj] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Mjesto] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Drzava] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Telefon] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Fax] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [eMail] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [OIB] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [NacinOtpreme] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [Rabat] [decimal](11, 2) NULL,
    [ZanemariAkciju] [int] NULL,
    [ZanemariRabatnu] [int] NULL,
    [LoyaltyKartica] [varchar](40) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [BodoviStanje] [int] NULL,
    [PostotakLoyaltyPopusta] [int] NULL,
    [Prioritet] [varchar](80) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [WandUserID] [int] NOT NULL DEFAULT (0),
    [SakrijKomercijalnePodatke] [bit] NOT NULL DEFAULT (0),
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Osobe_OsobaID] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED
(
    [OsobaID] ASC
) WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON)
)
END
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].[Kosaras]') AND type in (N'U'))
BEGIN
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Kosaras](
    [KosaraID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    [SifraKosare] [varchar](50) NULL,
    [NarudzbaID] [int] NOT NULL DEFAULT (0),
    [RobaID] [int] NULL,
    [Ident] [varchar](50) NULL,
    [Naziv] [varchar](200) NULL,
    [JM] [varchar](10) NULL,
    [VPCijena] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [MPCijena] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [Kolicina] [decimal](20, 3) NULL,
    [BrutoIznos] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [Rabat] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [IznosRabata] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [VPIznos] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [StopaPDV] [varchar](80) NULL DEFAULT (NULL),
    [IznosPDV] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [Ambalaza] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [Trosarina] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [MPIznos] [decimal](20, 2) NULL,
    [Izvor] [int] NULL DEFAULT (0),
    [PartnerID] [int] NOT NULL DEFAULT (0),
    [Napomena] [varchar](1000) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL,
    [DateCreated] [datetime] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Kosara_KosarID] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED
(
    [KosaraID] ASC
) WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
END
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','NarudzbaID') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje NarudzbaID u Kosaras dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras
            ADD NarudzbaID int NOT NULL DEFAULT (0) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','Ident') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polja Ident, Naziv i JM u Kosaras dodana!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Ident varchar(50) NULL DEFAULT ('-') WITH VALUES
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Naziv varchar(200) NULL DEFAULT ('Nedostupna roba') WITH VALUES
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD JM varchar(10) NULL DEFAULT ('kom') WITH VALUES
    END
GO
        UPDATE dbo.Kosaras
        SET Ident = robe.Ident, Naziv = robe.Naziv, JM = robe.JM
        FROM dbo.Robas as robe
        WHERE dbo.Kosaras.RobaID = robe.RobaID AND dbo.Kosaras.Ident = NULL
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','VPCijena') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polja VPCijena, MPCijena, Ambalaza, Trosarina u Kosaras dodana!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD VPCijena decimal(20,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT (0)
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD MPCijena decimal(20,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT (0)
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Ambalaza decimal(20,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT (0)
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Trosarina decimal(20,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT (0)
    END
GO
        UPDATE dbo.Kosaras
        SET VPCijena = VPIznos / ((1 - Rabat/100) * Kolicina), MPCijena = MPIznos / ((1 - Rabat/100) * Kolicina)
        WHERE VPCijena = 0 AND RobaID > 0 AND Kolicina !=0 AND Rabat !=100
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','Izvor') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje Izvor u Kosaras dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Izvor int NULL DEFAULT (0) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','Napomena') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'U tablicu Kosaras dodano polje Napomena!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD Napomena varchar(1000) COLLATE Croatian_CI_AS NULL
    END
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','PartnerID') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje PartnerID u Kosaras dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD PartnerID INT NOT NULL DEFAULT (0) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

IF ColumnProperty(object_id('dbo.Kosaras'), 'Ident', 'Precision') = 50
BEGIN
        Print 'Polje Ident u Kosaras prošireno na 80 karaktera!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ALTER COLUMN Ident varchar(80)
    END
GO

IF COL_LENGTH('Kosaras','StopaPDV') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje StopaPDV u Kosaras dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ADD StopaPDV varchar(80) NULL DEFAULT (NULL) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

IF ColumnProperty(object_id('dbo.Kosaras'), 'Kolicina', 'Scale') = 2
BEGIN
        Print 'Polje Kolicina u Kosaras prošireno na 3 decimale!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Kosaras ALTER COLUMN Kolicina decimal(20,3)
    END
GO

IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT * FROM sys.indexes WHERE name = 'ix_Pregled_starih_narudzbi' AND object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].[Kosaras]'))
BEGIN
        Print 'Kreiran index ix_Pregled_starih_narudzbi!'
        CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX [ix_Pregled_starih_narudzbi] ON [dbo].[Kosaras]
(
	[PartnerID] ASC,
	[SifraKosare] ASC
)

END
GO

(

) WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, DROP_EXISTING = OFF, ONLINE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON)
GO
IF COL_LENGTH('Narudzbas','OznakaDrzavePoreza') IS NULL
    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje ProdajaNaDaljinuEU u Narudzbas dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Narudzbas ADD [OznakaDrzavePoreza] [varchar](2) NULL DEFAULT (NULL) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

    BEGIN
        Print 'Polje Drzava u Narudzbas dodano!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Narudzbas ADD [Drzava] [varchar](2) NULL DEFAULT (NULL) WITH VALUES
    END
GO

BEGIN
        Print 'Polje Kolicina u Narudzbas prošireno na 3 decimale!'
        ALTER TABLE dbo.Narudzbas ALTER COLUMN Kolicina decimal(20,3)
    END
GO

BEGIN

END

/****** Object:  Table [dbo].[RobaCijenaDatums] Script Date: 31/03/2022 12:00:00 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].[RobaCijenaDatums]') AND type in (N'U'))
BEGIN
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[RobaCijenaDatums](
    [ID] [bigint] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    [RobaID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [Cijena] [decimal](11, 2) NOT NULL,
    [CijenaPrijePopusta] [decimal](11, 2) NOT NULL,
    [DatumStart] [datetime] NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_RobaCijenaDatums] PRIMARY KEY NONCLUSTERED
(
    [ID] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
CREATE UNIQUE CLUSTERED INDEX [ix_ID_RobaID] ON [dbo].[RobaCijenaDatums]
(
    [RobaID] ASC,
    [ID] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, DROP_EXISTING = OFF, ONLINE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].[CurrentPrices]') AND type in (N'V'))
EXEC('CREATE VIEW [dbo].[CurrentPrices] AS
    SELECT * FROM RobaCijenaDatums AS rcd
    WHERE rcd.ID = (SELECT MAX(ID) FROM RobaCijenaDatums AS rcd2 WHERE rcd2.RobaID = rcd.RobaID)')
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].[OldPrices]') AND type in (N'V'))
EXEC('CREATE VIEW [dbo].[OldPrices] AS
with Prices AS (
SELECT rcd.ID, rcd.RobaID, rcd.Cijena, rcd.CijenaPrijePopusta, rcd.DatumStart,
    LEAD(rcd.DatumStart,1,''9999-12-31'') OVER(PARTITION BY rcd.RobaID ORDER BY rcd.ID) AS DatumEnd,
    cp.DatumStart as CurrentPriceStart
    FROM RobaCijenaDatums AS rcd
    inner join CurrentPrices as cp on rcd.RobaID = cp.RobaID
    WHERE rcd.ID != cp.ID)
    select *,DATEDIFF(DAY,DatumEnd, CurrentPriceStart) AS DayDiff from Prices')
END
GO
